Table I: Potentiometric Indicators

| Dyes | Structure (Charge) | Optical Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ANEP dyes (aminonaphthyl-ethenylpyridinium) | Styryl (cationic or zwitterionic) | FAST; fluorescence excitation ratio 440/505 nm decreases upon membrane depolarization |
| RH dyes (Rina Hildesheim) | Styryl (cationic or zwitterionic) | FAST; generally similar to ANEP dyes with excitation red shift upon membrane hyperpolarization |
| Impermeant Oxonols (oxonol dyes with phenylsulfonate substituents) | Hybrid oxonol (anionic) | FAST; absorbance changes upon membrane hyperpolarization |
| Carbocyanines (Indo-DiI), thia (DiS) and oxa- (DiO) carbocyanines with short (n=1-7) alkyl tails | Carbocyanine (cationic) | SLOW; fluorescence generally decreases upon membrane hyperpolarization |
| Rhodamine and the methyl and ethyl esters of tetramethylrhodamine | Rhodamine (cationic) | SLOW; used to obtain unbiased images of potential-dependent dye distribution |
| Oxonols | Oxonol (anionic) | SLOW; fluorescence decreases upon membrane hyperpolarization |
| DiBAC Dyes (bis-barbituric acid oxonols) | Oxonol (anionic) | SLOW; fluorescence decreases upon membrane hyperpolarization |
